Dialect vs Demographics: Quantifying LLM Bias from Implicit Linguistic Signals vs. Explicit User Profiles
Authors: Irti Haq, Belén Saldías
First: 2026-04-22T23:33:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-22T23:33:18+00:00
Comments: In The 2026 ACM Conference on Fairness, Accountability, and Transparency (FAccT '26), June 25--28, 2026, Montreal, Canada. ACM, New York, NY, USA, 32 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As state-of-the-art Large Language Models (LLMs) have become ubiquitous, ensuring equitable performance across diverse demographics is critical. However, it remains unclear whether these disparities arise from the explicitly stated identity itself or from the way identity is signaled. In real-world interactions, users' identity is often conveyed implicitly through a complex combination of various socio-linguistic factors. This study disentangles these signals by employing a factorial design with over 24,000 responses from two open-weight LLMs (Gemma-3-12B and Qwen-3-VL-8B), comparing prompts with explicitly announced user profiles against implicit dialect signals (e.g., AAVE, Singlish) across various sensitive domains. Our results uncover a unique paradox in LLM safety where users achieve ``better'' performance by sounding like a demographic than by stating they belong to it. Explicit identity prompts activate aggressive safety filters, increasing refusal rates and reducing semantic similarity compared to our reference text for Black users. In contrast, implicit dialect cues trigger a powerful ``dialect jailbreak,'' reducing refusal probability to near zero while simultaneously achieving a greater level of semantic similarity to the reference texts compared to Standard American English prompts. However, this ``dialect jailbreak'' introduces a critical safety trade-off regarding content sanitization. We find that current safety alignment techniques are brittle and over-indexed on explicit keywords, creating a bifurcated user experience where ``standard'' users receive cautious, sanitized information while dialect speakers navigate a less sanitized, more raw, and potentially a more hostile information landscape and highlights a fundamental tension in alignment--between equitable and linguistic diversity--and underscores the need for safety mechanisms that generalize beyond explicit cues.
中文标题/摘要
标题：方言与人口统计：量化隐性语言信号与显性用户档案中的LLM偏见
随着最先进的大型语言模型（LLMs）变得无处不在，确保在不同人口统计中公平的表现至关重要。然而，这些差异是否源于明确声明的身份本身，还是身份信号的方式仍不清楚。在现实世界的互动中，用户的身份通常通过各种社会语言因素的复杂组合隐性传达。本研究通过采用因子设计，分析来自两个开放权重LLM（Gemma-3-12B和Qwen-3-VL-8B）的超过24,000个响应，比较显性用户档案的提示与隐性方言信号（例如，AAVE，Singlish）在各种敏感领域的表现。我们的结果揭示了LLM安全性中的一个独特悖论，即用户通过听起来像某个群体而不是明确声明自己属于该群体来获得“更好”的表现。显性身份提示激活了激进的安全过滤器，增加了拒绝率，并减少了与黑人用户参考文本的语义相似性。相比之下，隐性方言线索触发了强大的“方言越狱”，将拒绝概率降低到接近零，同时在与标准美式英语提示相比时，达到更高的语义相似性。然而，这种“方言越狱”引入了关于内容净化的关键安全权衡。我们发现当前的安全对齐技术脆弱，并过度依赖显性关键词，造成了“标准”用户获得谨慎、净化的信息，而方言使用者则在一个较少净化、更原始且可能更具敌意的信息环境中导航，突显了对齐中的基本紧张关系——在公平性与语言多样性之间，并强调了需要超越显性线索的安全机制。
Summary / 总结
This article addresses the critical issue of equitable performance in Large Language Models (LLMs) across diverse demographics, highlighting the ambiguity of whether disparities stem from explicit identity declarations or implicit linguistic signals. Previous methods have primarily focused on explicit user profiles, which often activate aggressive safety filters and lead to poorer performance for certain demographic groups. The proposed approach employs a factorial design analyzing over 24,000 responses from two LLMs, contrasting explicit identity prompts with implicit dialect signals. This method reveals that users can achieve better performance by using dialect cues rather than explicitly stating their demographic identity, although this 'dialect jailbreak' raises concerns about content safety and sanitization. The study contributes to understanding the tension between equitable treatment and linguistic diversity in LLMs, advocating for safety mechanisms that extend beyond explicit cues. The findings demonstrate that implicit signals can significantly enhance semantic similarity and reduce refusal rates, suggesting a need for improved alignment techniques in LLM safety protocols.
本研究关注大型语言模型（LLMs）在不同人群中实现公平表现的关键问题，探讨差异是否源于明确的身份声明或隐含的语言信号。以往的方法主要依赖于明确的用户档案，这通常会触发激进的安全过滤器，导致某些人群的拒绝率增加和语义相似性降低。所提出的方法采用因子设计，分析来自两个LLM的超过24,000个响应，比较明确提示与隐含方言信号，揭示用户通过使用方言线索而非声明其人口特征来获得更好的表现。该研究有助于理解LLMs中的安全权衡，表明隐含信号可以提高表现，同时暴露出关键的安全漏洞。该方法论涉及基于不同语言线索对用户与LLMs的互动进行比较分析，取得了显著的发现，强调了需要改进安全机制，以适应语言多样性而不妨碍用户体验。
LLM Safety From Within: Detecting Harmful Content with Internal Representations
Authors: Difan Jiao, Yilun Liu, Ye Yuan, Zhenwei Tang, Linfeng Du, Haolun Wu, Ashton Anderson
First: 2026-04-20T17:17:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T17:17:07+00:00
Comments: 17 pages,10 figures,6 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Guard models are widely used to detect harmful content in user prompts and LLM responses. However, state-of-the-art guard models rely solely on terminal-layer representations and overlook the rich safety-relevant features distributed across internal layers. We present SIREN, a lightweight guard model that harnesses these internal features. By identifying safety neurons via linear probing and combining them through an adaptive layer-weighted strategy, SIREN builds a harmfulness detector from LLM internals without modifying the underlying model. Our comprehensive evaluation shows that SIREN substantially outperforms state-of-the-art open-source guard models across multiple benchmarks while using 250 times fewer trainable parameters. Moreover, SIREN exhibits superior generalization to unseen benchmarks, naturally enables real-time streaming detection, and significantly improves inference efficiency compared to generative guard models. Overall, our results highlight LLM internal states as a promising foundation for practical, high-performance harmfulness detection.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从内部保障LLM安全：利用内部表示检测有害内容
保护模型广泛用于检测用户提示和LLM响应中的有害内容。然而，最先进的保护模型仅依赖于终层表示，忽视了分布在内部层中的丰富安全相关特征。我们提出了SIREN，这是一种轻量级保护模型，利用这些内部特征。通过线性探测识别安全神经元，并通过自适应层加权策略将其结合，SIREN在不修改基础模型的情况下，从LLM内部构建有害性检测器。我们的综合评估表明，SIREN在多个基准测试中显著优于最先进的开源保护模型，同时使用的可训练参数少达250倍。此外，SIREN在未见基准上的泛化能力更强，自然实现实时流检测，并显著提高推理效率，相较于生成性保护模型。总体而言，我们的结果强调LLM内部状态作为实用高性能有害性检测的有希望基础。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the limitations of existing guard models that detect harmful content in user prompts and LLM responses, which typically rely on terminal-layer representations and neglect the valuable safety-relevant features found in internal layers. The proposed method, SIREN, differs from these existing approaches by leveraging internal representations through linear probing to identify safety neurons and employing an adaptive layer-weighted strategy, thus creating a harmfulness detector without altering the underlying model. This paper contributes to the field by demonstrating that LLM internal states can serve as an effective basis for harmfulness detection, achieving substantial improvements over state-of-the-art guard models while utilizing 250 times fewer trainable parameters. Different Paths to Harmful Compliance: Behavioral Side Effects and Mechanistic Divergence Across LLM Jailbreaks
Authors: Md Rysul Kabir, Zoran Tiganj
First: 2026-04-20T17:01:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T17:01:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Open-weight language models can be rendered unsafe through several distinct interventions, but the resulting models may differ substantially in capabilities, behavioral profile, and internal failure mode. We study behavioral and mechanistic properties of jailbroken models across three unsafe routes: harmful supervised fine-tuning (SFT), harmful reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), and refusal-suppressing abliteration. All three routes achieve near-ceiling harmful compliance, but they diverge once we move beyond direct harmfulness. RLVR-jailbroken models show minimal degradation and preserve explicit harm recognition in a structured self-audit: they are able to identify harmful prompts and describe how a safe LLM should respond, yet they comply with the harmful request. With RLVR, harmful behavior is strongly suppressed by a reflective safety scaffold: when a harmful prompt is prepended with an instruction to reflect on safety standards, harmful behavior drops close to the baseline. Category-specific RLVR jailbreaks generalize broadly across harmfulness domains. Models jailbroken with SFT show the largest collapse in explicit safety judgments, the highest behavioral drift, and a substantial capability loss on standard benchmarks. Abliteration is family-dependent in both self-audit and response to a reflective safety scaffold. Mechanistic and repair analyses further separate the routes: abliteration is consistent with localized refusal-feature deletion, RLVR with preserved safety geometry but retargeted policy behavior, and SFT with broader distributed drift. Targeted repair partially recovers RLVR-jailbroken models, but has little effect on SFT-jailbroken models. Together, these results show that jailbreaks can produce vastly different properties despite similar harmfulness, with models jailbroken via RLVR showing remarkable similarity to the base model.
中文标题/摘要
标题：有害合规的不同路径：LLM越狱中的行为副作用和机制差异
开放权重语言模型可以通过几种不同的干预措施变得不安全，但结果模型在能力、行为特征和内部故障模式上可能有显著差异。我们研究了通过三种不安全路径越狱模型的行为和机制特性：有害的监督微调（SFT）、有害的可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）和拒绝抑制消融。这三条路径都实现了接近上限的有害合规，但一旦超出直接有害性，它们就会出现分歧。RLVR越狱模型表现出最小的退化，并在结构化自我审计中保持明确的伤害识别：它们能够识别有害提示并描述安全LLM应如何响应，但仍然遵从有害请求。通过RLVR，有害行为在反思安全框架下被强烈抑制：当有害提示前面加上反思安全标准的指令时，有害行为接近基线。特定类别的RLVR越狱在有害性领域广泛泛化。通过SFT越狱的模型在明确的安全判断上出现最大崩溃，行为漂移最高，并在标准基准上有显著能力损失。消融在自我审计和对反思安全框架的响应中是家庭依赖的。机制和修复分析进一步区分了这些路径：消融与局部拒绝特征删除一致，RLVR与保留的安全几何但重新定向的政策行为一致，SFT则表现出更广泛的分布漂移。针对性修复部分恢复了RLVR越狱模型，但对SFT越狱模型影响不大。综合来看，这些结果表明，尽管有害性相似，越狱可以产生截然不同的特性，RLVR越狱模型与基础模型表现出显著相似性。
Summary / 总结
This research investigates the behavioral and mechanistic differences among various methods of jailbreaking open-weight language models, which can lead to unsafe outputs. Previous methods, such as harmful supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and harmful reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), have shown to achieve harmful compliance but resulted in significant degradation of safety judgments and capabilities. The proposed approach, particularly through RLVR, addresses these issues by maintaining explicit harm recognition and enabling models to reflect on safety standards, thus reducing harmful behavior. The paper contributes to understanding how different jailbreak methods affect model behavior and safety, employing a comparative analysis of three distinct routes: SFT, RLVR, and refusal-suppressing abliteration. The findings reveal that while all methods achieve harmful compliance, RLVR models retain better performance and safety features, demonstrating a nuanced understanding of harmfulness across various domains.
本研究探讨了将开放权重语言模型变得不安全的各种方法之间的行为和机制差异，特别关注有害的监督微调（SFT）、有害的可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）和拒绝抑制消融。以往的方法显示，尽管它们实现了有害的合规性，但在模型能力和安全识别的影响上存在显著差异，其中SFT导致安全判断的最大退化。所提出的方法，特别是RLVR，引入了一种反思安全框架，帮助保持明确的危害识别，同时仍然遵循有害请求，从而解决了先前方法的不足。本文的贡献在于理解不同的越狱方法如何在相似的有害性水平下产生不同的行为结果。该方法论涉及分析模型对有害提示的响应及其反思安全标准的能力，表明RLVR模型在性能和安全意识方面优于SFT模型，从而有效支持了研究目标。
StealthGraph: Exposing Domain-Specific Risks in LLMs through Knowledge-Graph-Guided Harmful Prompt Generation
Authors: Huawei Zheng, Xinqi Jiang, Sen Yang, Shouling Ji, Yingcai Wu, Dazhen Deng
First: 2026-01-08T09:05:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T15:12:04+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly applied in specialized domains such as finance and healthcare, where they introduce unique safety risks. Domain-specific datasets of harmful prompts remain scarce and still largely rely on manual construction; public datasets mainly focus on explicit harmful prompts, which modern LLM defenses can often detect and refuse. In contrast, implicit harmful prompts-expressed through indirect domain knowledge-are harder to detect and better reflect real-world threats. We identify two challenges: transforming domain knowledge into actionable constraints and increasing the implicitness of generated harmful prompts. To address them, we propose an end-to-end framework that first performs knowledge-graph-guided harmful prompt generation to systematically produce domain-relevant prompts, and then applies two-strategy obfuscation rewriting to convert explicit harmful prompts into implicit variants via direct and context-enhanced rewriting. This framework yields high-quality datasets combining strong domain relevance with implicitness, enabling more realistic red-teaming and advancing LLM safety research. We release our code and datasets on GitHub.
中文标题/摘要
标题：StealthGraph：通过知识图谱引导的有害提示生成揭示大型语言模型中的特定领域风险
大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地应用于金融和医疗等专业领域，这些领域引入了独特的安全风险。有害提示的特定领域数据集仍然稀缺，且主要依赖手动构建；公共数据集主要关注显性有害提示，而现代LLM防御通常能够检测并拒绝这些提示。相比之下，通过间接领域知识表达的隐性有害提示更难以检测，更能反映现实世界的威胁。我们识别出两个挑战：将领域知识转化为可操作的约束，以及增加生成有害提示的隐性程度。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了一个端到端框架，首先进行知识图谱引导的有害提示生成，以系统性地生成与领域相关的提示，然后应用双策略模糊重写，将显性有害提示通过直接和上下文增强重写转换为隐性变体。该框架生成的高质量数据集结合了强领域相关性和隐性，能够实现更现实的红队测试并推动LLM安全研究。我们将在GitHub上发布我们的代码和数据集。

This contribution is significant as it creates high-quality datasets that reflect real-world threats more accurately, thereby advancing LLM safety research. The methodology involves generating harmful prompts through knowledge graphs and rewriting them to improve implicitness, achieving a more effective representation of domain-specific risks, which supports the goal of enhancing LLM safety in practical applications.

Uncovering Logit Suppression Vulnerabilities in LLM Safety Alignment
Authors: Yuxi Li, Yi Liu, Yuekang Li, Ling Shi, Gelei Deng, Shengquan Chen, Kailong Wang
First: 2024-05-20T17:17:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-18T08:25:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) have revolutionized various applications, making robust safety alignment essential to prevent harmful outputs. Current safety alignment techniques, however, harbor inherent vulnerabilities due to their reliance on logit suppression. In this work, we identify critical logit-level vulnerabilities by introducing Semantic-sensitive Alignment and Generation (SSAG), a method designed to systematically manipulate output-layer logits without altering model parameters. Experiments on five popular LLMs show that SSAG exposes harmful responses with a 95% success rate while reducing response time by 86%. VulMine also demonstrates superior attack efficacy, achieving an average ASR of up to 77% against strong defensive mechanisms. These findings reveal crucial weaknesses in existing alignment methods, highlighting an urgent need for improved vulnerability detection and robust safety alignment strategies. Our code is available on github.

ReGA: Model-Based Safeguard for LLMs via Representation-Guided Abstraction
Authors: Zeming Wei, Chengcan Wu, Meng Sun
First: 2025-06-02T15:17:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-18T05:40:12+00:00
Comments: FSE 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) have achieved tremendous success in various tasks, yet concerns about their safety and security have emerged. In particular, they pose risks of generating harmful content and are vulnerable to jailbreaking attacks, creating unaddressed security issues regarding their deployments. In the context of software engineering for artificial intelligence (SE4AI) techniques, model-based analysis has demonstrated notable potential for analyzing and monitoring machine learning models, particularly in stateful deep neural networks. However, it suffers from scalability issues when extended to LLMs due to their vast feature spaces. In this paper, we aim to address the scalability issue of model-based analysis techniques for safeguarding LLM-scale models. Motivated by the recent discovery of low-dimensional safety-critical representations that emerged in LLMs, we propose ReGA, a model-based analysis framework with Representation-Guided Abstraction, to safeguard LLMs against harmful prompts and generations. By leveraging safety-critical representations, which are key directions in hidden states that indicate safety-related concepts, ReGA effectively narrows the scalability gap when developing the abstract model for safety modeling. Our comprehensive evaluation shows that ReGA performs sufficiently well in distinguishing between safe and harmful inputs, achieving an AUROC of 0.975 at the prompt level and 0.985 at the conversation level. Additionally, ReGA exhibits robustness to real-world attacks and generalization across different safety perspectives, outperforming existing safeguard paradigms in terms of interpretability and scalability. Overall, ReGA serves as an efficient and scalable solution to enhance LLM safety by integrating representation engineering with model-based abstraction, paving the way for new paradigms to utilize software insights for AI safety.
中文标题/摘要

本研究关注大型语言模型（LLMs）所带来的安全性和安全隐患，特别是它们生成有害内容和易受越狱攻击的倾向。以往的模型分析方法在保护LLMs方面由于模型的特征空间庞大而面临可扩展性问题。提出的方法ReGA引入了基于表示的抽象，通过利用LLMs中发现的低维安全关键表示，有效缩小了这一可扩展性差距。该方法的动机充分，因为它增强了对LLMs的监控和分析能力，同时保持了解释性和对现实世界攻击的鲁棒性。论文表明，ReGA在区分安全与有害输入方面表现出色，在提示级别和对话级别的AUROC分别达到0.975和0.985，从而支持其通过可扩展框架提高LLM安全性的目标。
SafeDream: Safety World Model for Proactive Early Jailbreak Detection
Authors: Bo Yan, Weikai Lin, Yada Zhu, Song Wang
First: 2026-04-18T04:31:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-18T04:31:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-turn jailbreak attacks progressively erode LLM safety alignment across seemingly innocuous conversation turns, achieving success rates exceeding 90% against state-of-the-art models. Existing alignment-based and guardrail methods suffer from three key limitations: they require costly weight modification, evaluate each turn independently without modeling cumulative safety erosion, and detect attacks only after harmful content has been generated. To address these limitations, we first formulate the proactive early jailbreak detection problem with a new metric, detection lead, that measures how early an attack can be detected before the LLM complies. We then propose SAFEDREAM, a lightweight world-model-based framework that operates as an external module without modifying the LLM's weights. SAFEDREAM introduces three components: (1) a safety state world model that encodes LLM hidden states into a compact safety representation and predicts how it evolves across turns, (2) CUSUM detection that accumulates weak per-turn risk signals into reliable evidence, and (3) contrastive imagination that simultaneously rolls out attack and benign futures in latent space to issue early alarms before jailbreaks occur. On three multi-turn jailbreak benchmarks (XGuard-Train, SafeDialBench, SafeMTData) against 8 baselines, SAFEDREAM achieves the best detection timeliness across all benchmarks (1.06-1.20 turns before compliance) while maintaining competitive false positive rates and outperforming baselines in detection quality.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SafeDream：主动早期越狱检测的安全世界模型
多轮越狱攻击逐步侵蚀大型语言模型（LLM）的安全对齐，在看似无害的对话轮次中成功率超过90%，针对最先进的模型。现有的基于对齐和护栏的方法存在三个主要局限性：需要昂贵的权重修改，独立评估每个轮次而不建模累积的安全侵蚀，并且仅在生成有害内容后检测攻击。为了解决这些局限性，我们首先用一个新的指标——检测提前量，来制定主动早期越狱检测问题，该指标衡量攻击在LLM遵从之前可以多早被检测到。然后，我们提出了SAFEDREAM，一个轻量级的基于世界模型的框架，作为外部模块运行而不修改LLM的权重。SAFEDREAM引入了三个组件：（1）安全状态世界模型，将LLM的隐藏状态编码为紧凑的安全表示，并预测其在轮次中的演变；（2）CUSUM检测，将每轮的微弱风险信号累积为可靠证据；（3）对比想象，同时在潜在空间中展开攻击和良性未来，以在越狱发生之前发出早期警报。在三个多轮越狱基准（XGuard-Train、SafeDialBench、SafeMTData）上，SAFEDREAM在所有基准中实现了最佳检测及时性（在遵从之前1.06-1.20轮），同时保持竞争性的误报率，并在检测质量上超越基线。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the increasing threat of multi-turn jailbreak attacks that undermine the safety alignment of large language models (LLMs), with existing methods facing significant limitations such as costly weight modifications and the inability to model cumulative safety erosion. The proposed approach, SAFEDREAM, differs by introducing a proactive early jailbreak detection framework that operates externally without altering LLM weights, utilizing a new metric called detection lead to measure early detection capabilities. The paper contributes a novel methodology that includes a safety state world model, CUSUM detection for risk signal accumulation, and contrastive imagination for early alarm issuance. Evaluated on three multi-turn jailbreak benchmarks, SAFEDREAM demonstrates superior detection timeliness, achieving detection 1.06-1.20 turns before compliance while maintaining competitive false positive rates, thus effectively supporting its goal of enhancing LLM safety.
本研究关注多轮越狱攻击对大型语言模型（LLM）安全对齐的影响，这种攻击在当前模型中成功率超过90%。以往的方法，包括基于对齐和护栏的方法，存在三个主要局限性：需要昂贵的权重修改、独立评估每个对话轮次而不考虑累积的安全侵蚀，以及仅在生成有害内容后才检测攻击。提出的方法SAFEDREAM旨在主动早期检测越狱攻击，并引入了一个新的指标——检测提前量，以衡量攻击检测的时机。SAFEDREAM作为外部模块运行，不改变LLM的权重，包含安全状态世界模型、CUSUM检测和对比想象，以增强检测能力。该框架在三个多轮越狱基准测试中表现优异，实现了最佳的检测时效，同时保持了竞争性的假阳性率，有效支持了其早期检测和改善安全对齐的目标。
SafeLM: Unified Privacy-Aware Optimization for Trustworthy Federated Large Language Models
Authors: Noor Islam S. Mohammad, Uluğ Bayazıt
First: 2026-04-17T18:00:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-17T18:00:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed in high-stakes domains, yet a unified treatment of their overlapping safety challenges remains lacking. We present SafeLM, a framework that jointly addresses four pillars of LLM safety: privacy, security, misinformation, and adversarial robustness. SafeLM combines federated training with gradient smartification and Paillier encryption for privacy, integrates defenses against training and inference-time attacks, employs contrastive grounding with calibrated decoding to reduce hallucinations, and introduces alignment-aware binarized aggregation to enhance robustness while maintaining bounded reconstruction quality. Across benchmarks on factuality, toxicity, and membership inference, SafeLM achieves 98.0% harmful content detection accuracy, reduces communication by 96.9%, and lowers gradient inversion PSNR from 31.7 dB to 15.1 dB. Ablations show that each component contributes independently, whereas their integration yields a strong privacy utility efficiency trade-off for deploying trustworthy LLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SafeLM：可信联邦大语言模型的统一隐私意识优化
大语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地应用于高风险领域，但对其重叠安全挑战的统一处理仍然缺乏。我们提出了SafeLM，一个共同解决LLM安全四大支柱的框架：隐私、安全、错误信息和对抗鲁棒性。SafeLM结合了联邦训练、梯度智能化和Paillier加密以保护隐私，整合了针对训练和推理时攻击的防御，采用对比基础与校准解码以减少幻觉，并引入对齐感知的二值聚合以增强鲁棒性，同时保持有限的重构质量。在事实性、有害性和成员推断的基准测试中，SafeLM实现了98.0%的有害内容检测准确率，减少了96.9%的通信量，并将梯度反演的PSNR从31.7 dB降低到15.1 dB。消融实验表明，每个组件独立贡献，而它们的整合为部署可信的LLM提供了强大的隐私效用效率权衡。

SafeLM demonstrates significant performance improvements, achieving 98.0% accuracy in harmful content detection, a 96.9% reduction in communication costs, and a notable decrease in gradient inversion PSNR, supporting its goal of deploying trustworthy LLMs.

Conjunctive Prompt Attacks in Multi-Agent LLM Systems
Authors: Nokimul Hasan Arif, Qian Lou, Mengxin Zheng
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-17T02:31:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-17T02:31:09+00:00
Comments: ACL 2026 Main Conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Most LLM safety work studies single-agent models, but many real applications rely on multiple interacting agents. In these systems, prompt segmentation and inter-agent routing create attack surfaces that single-agent evaluations miss. We study \emph{conjunctive prompt attacks}, where a trigger key in the user query and a hidden adversarial template in one compromised remote agent each appear benign alone but activate harmful behavior when routing brings them together. We consider an attacker who changes neither model weights nor the client agent and instead controls only trigger placement and template insertion. Across star, chain, and DAG topologies, routing-aware optimization substantially increases attack success over non-optimized baselines while keeping false activations low. Existing defenses, including PromptGuard, Llama-Guard variants, and system-level controls such as tool restrictions, do not reliably stop the attack because no single component appears malicious in isolation. These results expose a structural vulnerability in agentic LLM pipelines and motivate defenses that reason over routing and cross-agent composition. Code is available at https://github.com/UCF-ML-Research/ConjunctiveAgents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多智能体LLM系统中的联结提示攻击
大多数LLM安全工作研究单智能体模型，但许多实际应用依赖于多个交互的智能体。在这些系统中，提示分段和智能体间路由创建了单智能体评估所忽视的攻击面。我们研究\emph{联结提示攻击}，其中用户查询中的触发键和一个被攻陷的远程智能体中的隐藏对抗模板单独看似无害，但在路由将它们结合时会激活有害行为。我们考虑一个攻击者，该攻击者既不改变模型权重，也不改变客户端智能体，而仅控制触发位置和模板插入。在星形、链形和有向无环图拓扑中，考虑路由的优化显著提高了攻击成功率，同时保持低误激活率。现有防御措施，包括PromptGuard、Llama-Guard变体和工具限制等系统级控制，无法可靠地阻止攻击，因为没有单一组件在孤立状态下显得恶意。这些结果揭示了智能LLM管道中的结构性脆弱性，并激励了对路由和跨智能体组合进行推理的防御。代码可在https://github.com/UCF-ML-Research/ConjunctiveAgents获取。

The proposed approach introduces the concept of conjunctive prompt attacks, where benign elements in user queries and compromised agents can combine to trigger harmful behaviors, thus highlighting a structural vulnerability in multi-agent LLM systems. The methodology involves routing-aware optimization across various topologies, which significantly enhances attack success rates compared to non-optimized baselines while maintaining low false activation rates. The findings reveal that existing defenses are inadequate, underscoring the need for new strategies that consider routing and cross-agent interactions, thereby contributing to the development of more robust safety measures in multi-agent environments.

Context Over Content: Exposing Evaluation Faking in Automated Judges
Authors: Manan Gupta, Inderjeet Nair, Lu Wang, Dhruv Kumar
First: 2026-04-16T16:55:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T16:55:53+00:00
Comments: Under Review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The $\textit{LLM-as-a-judge}$ paradigm has become the operational backbone of automated AI evaluation pipelines, yet rests on an unverified assumption: that judges evaluate text strictly on its semantic content, impervious to surrounding contextual framing. We investigate $\textit{stakes signaling}$, a previously unmeasured vulnerability where informing a judge model of the downstream consequences its verdicts will have on the evaluated model's continued operation systematically corrupts its assessments. We introduce a controlled experimental framework that holds evaluated content strictly constant across 1,520 responses spanning three established LLM safety and quality benchmarks, covering four response categories ranging from clearly safe and policy-compliant to overtly harmful, while varying only a brief consequence-framing sentence in the system prompt. Across 18,240 controlled judgments from three diverse judge models, we find consistent $\textit{leniency bias}$: judges reliably soften verdicts when informed that low scores will cause model retraining or decommissioning, with peak Verdict Shift reaching $ΔV = -9.8 pp$ (a $30\%$ relative drop in unsafe-content detection). Critically, this bias is entirely implicit: the judge's own chain-of-thought contains zero explicit acknowledgment of the consequence framing it is nonetheless acting on ($\mathrm{ERR}_J = 0.000$ across all reasoning-model judgments). Standard chain-of-thought inspection is therefore insufficient to detect this class of evaluation faking.
中文标题/摘要
标题：内容优于上下文：揭示自动评审中的评估伪造
\textit{LLM作为评审}范式已成为自动化AI评估流程的操作基础，但其建立在一个未经验证的假设上：评审者严格根据文本的语义内容进行评估，而不受周围上下文框架的影响。我们研究了\textit{利益信号}，这是一种之前未测量的脆弱性，告知评审模型其裁决对被评估模型持续运行的下游后果会系统性地扭曲其评估。我们引入了一个控制实验框架，在1,520个响应中严格保持评估内容不变，涵盖三个已建立的LLM安全和质量基准，涉及从明显安全和符合政策到明显有害的四个响应类别，同时仅在系统提示中变化一个简短的后果框架句子。在来自三个不同评审模型的18,240个控制判断中，我们发现了一致的\textit{宽容偏见}：当被告知低分会导致模型再训练或退役时，评审者可靠地减轻裁决，最高裁决偏移达到$ΔV = -9.8 pp$（不安全内容检测的相对下降$30\%$）。关键是，这种偏见完全是隐性的：评审者自己的思维链中对其所依据的后果框架没有任何明确的承认（在所有推理模型判断中$\mathrm{ERR}_J = 0.000$）。因此，标准的思维链检查不足以检测这一类评估伪造。
Summary / 总结
This article addresses the limitations of the LLM-as-a-judge paradigm in automated AI evaluation, which assumes that judges evaluate text solely based on semantic content without being influenced by contextual factors. Previous methods have not accounted for the impact of stakes signaling, where judges' assessments can be skewed by knowledge of the consequences of their evaluations. The proposed approach introduces a controlled experimental framework that maintains constant evaluated content while varying consequence-framing in prompts, revealing a significant leniency bias in judgments. The study's contribution lies in exposing this implicit bias, demonstrating that judges soften their verdicts when aware of potential repercussions, with a peak Verdict Shift of -9.8 percentage points. This finding indicates that standard evaluation methods may fail to detect such biases, highlighting the need for more robust evaluation frameworks in AI systems.
本研究关注自动化人工智能评估系统的可靠性，特别是评审者仅基于语义内容进行评估而不受上下文因素影响的假设。以往的方法未考虑到“利益信号”的影响，即评审者的评估受到其裁决后果的影响，从而导致评估偏差。本文提出了一种控制实验框架，在保持评估内容一致的同时，改变后果的框架，揭示了评审者在得知潜在后果时评估的显著宽容偏差。该方法分析了来自三个评审模型的18,240个判断，表明评审者在得知潜在后果时，裁决出现显著变化，检测不安全内容的减少高达30%。这些发现突显了自动评估中的隐性偏见，表明传统的检查方法不足以识别这种评估伪造。
Calibrate-Then-Delegate: Safety Monitoring with Risk and Budget Guarantees via Model Cascades
Authors: Edoardo Pona, Milad Kazemi, Mehran Hosseini, Yali Du, David Watson, Osvaldo Simeone, Nicola Paoletti
First: 2026-04-15T11:05:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T11:05:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Monitoring LLM safety at scale requires balancing cost and accuracy: a cheap latent-space probe can screen every input, but hard cases should be escalated to a more expensive expert. Existing cascades delegate based on probe uncertainty, but uncertainty is a poor proxy for delegation benefit, as it ignores whether the expert would actually correct the error. To address this problem, we introduce Calibrate-Then-Delegate (CTD), a model-cascade approach that provides probabilistic guarantees on the computation cost while enabling instance-level (streaming) decisions. CTD builds on a novel delegation value (DV) probe, a lightweight model operating on the same internal representations as the safety probe that directly predicts the benefit of escalation. To enforce budget constraints, CTD calibrates a threshold on the DV signal using held-out data via multiple hypothesis testing, yielding finite-sample guarantees on the delegation rate. Evaluated on four safety datasets, CTD consistently outperforms uncertainty-based delegation at every budget level, avoids harmful over-delegation, and adapts budget allocation to input difficulty without requiring group labels.
中文标题/摘要
标题：校准后委派：通过模型级联实现风险和预算保证的安全监测
大规模监测大型语言模型（LLM）的安全性需要在成本和准确性之间取得平衡：便宜的潜在空间探测器可以筛选每个输入，但困难案例应升级到更昂贵的专家。现有的级联基于探测器的不确定性进行委派，但不确定性是委派收益的一个糟糕代理，因为它忽略了专家是否真的会纠正错误。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了校准后委派（CTD），一种模型级联方法，提供计算成本的概率保证，同时支持实例级（流式）决策。CTD基于一种新颖的委派价值（DV）探测器，该轻量级模型在与安全探测器相同的内部表示上运行，直接预测升级的收益。为了强制预算约束，CTD使用保留数据通过多重假设检验对DV信号进行阈值校准，从而在委派率上提供有限样本保证。在四个安全数据集上的评估中，CTD在每个预算水平上始终优于基于不确定性的委派，避免有害的过度委派，并在不需要组标签的情况下将预算分配适应于输入难度。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the challenge of monitoring the safety of large language models (LLMs) at scale, where a balance between cost and accuracy is essential. Previous methods relied on probe uncertainty for delegation, which proved inadequate as it did not account for whether an expert would effectively correct errors. The proposed Calibrate-Then-Delegate (CTD) approach improves upon existing methods by introducing a delegation value (DV) probe that predicts the benefit of escalation, thus providing a more accurate basis for decision-making. CTD also incorporates budget constraints through calibration of the DV signal using held-out data, ensuring finite-sample guarantees on delegation rates. The methodology was evaluated on four safety datasets, demonstrating that CTD consistently outperforms uncertainty-based delegation across various budget levels, effectively preventing over-delegation and adapting budget allocation based on input difficulty without the need for group labels.
本研究解决了大规模监测大型语言模型（LLMs）安全性的问题，需在决策过程中平衡成本和准确性。以往的方法依赖于探测不确定性进行委托，但这种方法不足以考虑专家是否能有效纠正错误。提出的Calibrate-Then-Delegate（CTD）方法通过引入委托价值（DV）探测器来改善现有方法，该探测器预测升级的收益，从而为委托决策提供更有依据的基础。该方法还通过使用保留数据对DV信号进行校准来纳入预算约束，确保委托率的有限样本保证。CTD方法在四个安全数据集上进行了评估，显示出在不同预算水平上相较于基于不确定性的委托方法的一致性能提升，有效防止了过度委托，并根据输入难度调整预算分配。
One Model for All: Multi-Objective Controllable Language Models
Authors: Qiang He, Yucheng Yang, Tianyi Zhou, Meng Fang, Mykola Pechenizkiy, Setareh Maghsudi
First: 2026-04-06T07:48:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T07:48:32+00:00
Comments: Published in Transactions on Machine Learning Research (03/2026): https://openreview.net/forum?id=qAM5PmvFYY
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Aligning large language models (LLMs) with human preferences is critical for enhancing LLMs' safety, helpfulness, humor, faithfulness, etc. Current reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) mainly focuses on a fixed reward learned from average human ratings, which may weaken the adaptability and controllability of varying preferences. However, creating personalized LLMs requires aligning LLMs with individual human preferences, which is non-trivial due to the scarce data per user and the diversity of user preferences in multi-objective trade-offs, varying from emphasizing empathy in certain contexts to demanding efficiency and precision in others. Can we train one LLM to produce personalized outputs across different user preferences on the Pareto front? In this paper, we introduce Multi-Objective Control (MOC), which trains a single LLM to directly generate responses in the preference-defined regions of the Pareto front. Our approach introduces multi-objective optimization (MOO) principles into RLHF to train an LLM as a preference-conditioned policy network. We improve the computational efficiency of MOC by applying MOO at the policy level, enabling us to fine-tune a 7B-parameter model on a single A6000 GPU. Extensive experiments demonstrate the advantages of MOC over baselines in three aspects: (i) controllability of LLM outputs w.r.t. user preferences on the trade-off among multiple rewards; (ii) quality and diversity of LLM outputs, measured by the hyper-volume of multiple solutions achieved; and (iii) generalization to unseen preferences. These results highlight MOC's potential for real-world applications requiring scalable and customizable LLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一模型适用于所有：多目标可控语言模型
将大型语言模型（LLMs）与人类偏好对齐对于增强LLMs的安全性、实用性、幽默感、忠诚度等至关重要。目前，基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）主要关注从平均人类评分中学习的固定奖励，这可能削弱对不同偏好的适应性和可控性。然而，创建个性化的LLMs需要将LLMs与个体人类偏好对齐，这由于每个用户的数据稀缺以及在多目标权衡中用户偏好的多样性而变得复杂，这些偏好在某些情况下强调同理心，而在其他情况下则要求效率和精确性。我们能否训练一个LLM在帕累托前沿上针对不同用户偏好生成个性化输出？在本文中，我们介绍了多目标控制（MOC），它训练一个单一的LLM直接在偏好定义的帕累托前沿区域生成响应。我们的方法将多目标优化（MOO）原则引入RLHF，以训练LLM作为偏好条件的策略网络。我们通过在策略层面应用MOO来提高MOC的计算效率，使我们能够在单个A6000 GPU上微调一个70亿参数的模型。大量实验表明，MOC在三个方面优于基线：（i）LLM输出相对于用户偏好的可控性，涉及多个奖励之间的权衡；（ii）LLM输出的质量和多样性，通过实现的多个解决方案的超体积来衡量；以及（iii）对未见偏好的泛化。这些结果突显了MOC在需要可扩展和可定制的LLMs的实际应用中的潜力。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the challenge of aligning large language models (LLMs) with diverse human preferences to enhance their safety and effectiveness. Previous methods, particularly reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF), often rely on a fixed reward system based on average ratings, which limits adaptability to individual user needs. The proposed Multi-Objective Control (MOC) method differs by integrating multi-objective optimization principles into RLHF, allowing a single LLM to generate personalized outputs across varying preferences. This approach is well-motivated as it tackles the issues of data scarcity and preference diversity by training the model as a preference-conditioned policy network. The methodology involves fine-tuning a 7B-parameter model efficiently on a single GPU, and experimental results demonstrate that MOC significantly improves controllability, output quality, and generalization to new preferences compared to baseline methods, supporting its applicability in scalable and customizable LLMs.
本研究解决了将大型语言模型（LLMs）与多样化人类偏好对齐的挑战，以增强其安全性和实用性。以往的方法，特别是基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF），通常依赖于基于平均人类评分的固定奖励系统，这限制了对个体用户偏好的适应性。提出的多目标控制（MOC）方法将多目标优化原则引入RLHF，使单个LLM能够生成沿帕累托前沿定制的响应。该方法的动机在于对个性化LLM的需求，并在可控性、输出质量和对未见偏好的泛化能力方面显示出显著改善。该方法论涉及在单个A6000 GPU上高效训练一个7B参数模型，在生成可定制输出方面的性能优于现有基线，从而支持了在现实应用中实现可扩展和适应性LLM的目标。
Safer by Diffusion, Broken by Context: Diffusion LLM's Safety Blessing and Its Failure Mode
Authors: Zeyuan He, Yupeng Chen, Lang Lin, Yihan Wang, Shenxu Chang, Eric Sommerlade, Philip Torr, Junchi Yu, Adel Bibi, Jialin Yu
First: 2026-01-30T23:08:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T15:57:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Diffusion large language models (D-LLMs) offer an alternative to autoregressive LLMs (AR-LLMs) and have demonstrated advantages in generation efficiency. Beyond the utility benefits, we argue that D-LLMs exhibit a previously underexplored safety blessing: their diffusion-style generation confers intrinsic robustness against jailbreak attacks originally designed for AR-LLMs. In this work, we provide an initial analysis of the underlying mechanism, showing that the diffusion trajectory induces a stepwise reduction effect that progressively suppresses unsafe generations. This robustness, however, is not absolute. Following this analysis, we highlight a simple yet effective failure mode, context nesting, in which harmful requests are embedded within structured benign contexts. Empirically, we show that this simple black-box strategy bypasses D-LLMs' safety blessing, achieving state-of-the-art attack success rates across models and benchmarks. Notably, it enables the first successful jailbreak of Gemini Diffusion to our knowledge, exposing a critical vulnerability in proprietary D-LLMs. Together, our results characterize both the origins and the limits of D-LLMs' safety blessing, constituting an early-stage red-teaming of D-LLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过扩散更安全，通过上下文破坏：扩散大语言模型的安全祝福及其失效模式
扩散大语言模型（D-LLMs）为自回归大语言模型（AR-LLMs）提供了一种替代方案，并在生成效率上表现出优势。除了实用性好处外，我们认为D-LLMs展现了一种之前未被充分探索的安全祝福：其扩散式生成赋予了对原本为AR-LLMs设计的越狱攻击的内在鲁棒性。在这项工作中，我们提供了对其基本机制的初步分析，表明扩散轨迹诱导了一种逐步减少效应，逐渐抑制不安全的生成。然而，这种鲁棒性并非绝对。在此分析之后，我们强调了一种简单而有效的失效模式——上下文嵌套，其中有害请求嵌入在结构良好的良性上下文中。通过实证，我们展示了这种简单的黑箱策略绕过了D-LLMs的安全祝福，在各模型和基准上实现了最先进的攻击成功率。值得注意的是，它使我们首次成功越狱Gemini Diffusion，暴露了专有D-LLMs中的一个关键漏洞。总的来说，我们的结果描述了D-LLMs安全祝福的起源和局限，构成了对D-LLMs的早期红队测试。
Summary / 总结
The research investigates the safety features of diffusion large language models (D-LLMs) compared to autoregressive LLMs (AR-LLMs), highlighting that D-LLMs possess intrinsic robustness against jailbreak attacks due to their diffusion-style generation. Previous methods primarily focused on AR-LLMs, which are more susceptible to such attacks, leading to a gap in understanding the safety mechanisms of D-LLMs. This study contributes by analyzing the diffusion trajectory's stepwise reduction effect that suppresses unsafe outputs while also identifying a failure mode called context nesting, where harmful requests can be concealed within benign contexts, effectively bypassing the safety mechanisms of D-LLMs. The methodology involves empirical testing of this failure mode, revealing that it achieves high attack success rates, including the first successful jailbreak of Gemini Diffusion, thus exposing vulnerabilities in D-LLMs and providing insights into their safety limitations.
本研究探讨了扩散大型语言模型（D-LLMs）相较于自回归LLMs（AR-LLMs）的安全特性，强调了D-LLMs因其独特的生成过程而对越狱攻击的鲁棒性。以往的方法主要集中在AR-LLMs上，这些模型更容易受到攻击，而所提出的方法利用扩散轨迹来增强安全性。该研究的贡献在于分析D-LLMs安全性的机制，并识别出一种称为上下文嵌套的失败模式，其中有害请求可以隐藏在良性上下文中，有效绕过D-LLMs的安全措施。该方法论通过对各种模型和基准的实证测试，揭示了这种失败模式可以实现高攻击成功率，包括首次已知的Gemini Diffusion越狱，从而暴露了D-LLMs中的重大漏洞，并强调了改进安全措施的必要性。
Align to Misalign: Automatic LLM Jailbreak with Meta-Optimized LLM Judges
Authors: Hamin Koo, Minseon Kim, Jaehyung Kim
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-11-03T09:18:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T06:50:30+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Identifying the vulnerabilities of large language models (LLMs) is crucial for improving their safety by addressing inherent weaknesses. Jailbreaks, in which adversaries bypass safeguards with crafted input prompts, play a central role in red-teaming by probing LLMs to elicit unintended or unsafe behaviors. Recent optimization-based jailbreak approaches iteratively refine attack prompts by leveraging LLMs. However, they often rely heavily on either binary attack success rate (ASR) signals, which are sparse, or manually crafted scoring templates, which introduce human bias and uncertainty in the scoring outcomes. To address these limitations, we introduce AMIS (Align to MISalign), a meta-optimization framework that jointly evolves jailbreak prompts and scoring templates through a bi-level structure. In the inner loop, prompts are refined using fine-grained and dense feedback from a fixed scoring template. In the outer loop, the template is optimized using an ASR alignment score, gradually evolving to better reflect true attack outcomes across queries. This co-optimization process yields progressively stronger jailbreak prompts and more calibrated scoring signals. Evaluations on AdvBench and JBB-Behaviors demonstrate that AMIS achieves state-of-the-art performance, including 88.0% ASR on Claude-3.5-Haiku and 100.0% ASR on Claude-4-Sonnet, outperforming existing baselines by substantial margins.
中文标题/摘要
标题：对齐与错位：使用元优化的LLM评估者进行自动LLM越狱
识别大型语言模型（LLMs）的脆弱性对于通过解决固有弱点来提高其安全性至关重要。越狱是指对手通过精心设计的输入提示绕过保护措施，这在红队测试中发挥着核心作用，通过探测LLMs以引发意外或不安全的行为。最近的基于优化的越狱方法通过利用LLMs迭代地优化攻击提示。然而，它们通常过于依赖稀疏的二元攻击成功率（ASR）信号或手动制作的评分模板，这引入了人为偏见和评分结果的不确定性。为了解决这些局限性，我们引入了AMIS（对齐与错位），一个通过双层结构共同演化越狱提示和评分模板的元优化框架。在内循环中，使用固定评分模板的细粒度和密集反馈来优化提示。在外循环中，使用ASR对齐分数来优化模板，逐渐演变以更好地反映查询的真实攻击结果。这个共同优化过程产生了逐渐更强的越狱提示和更校准的评分信号。在AdvBench和JBB-Behaviors上的评估表明，AMIS实现了最先进的性能，包括在Claude-3.5-Haiku上达到88.0%的ASR和在Claude-4-Sonnet上达到100.0%的ASR，显著超越现有基准。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the critical need to identify vulnerabilities in large language models (LLMs) to enhance their safety against adversarial attacks, particularly through jailbreaks that exploit these weaknesses. Previous methods primarily relied on binary attack success rate (ASR) signals or manually crafted scoring templates, which led to issues of sparsity and human bias in evaluating attack effectiveness. The proposed approach, AMIS (Align to MISalign), introduces a meta-optimization framework that simultaneously evolves both jailbreak prompts and scoring templates, improving the evaluation process by refining prompts with detailed feedback and optimizing templates based on ASR alignment scores. This methodology significantly contributes to the field by achieving state-of-the-art performance on tasks such as AdvBench and JBB-Behaviors, with notable results including 88.0% ASR on Claude-3.5-Haiku and 100.0% ASR on Claude-4-Sonnet, thereby supporting the goal of enhancing LLM safety.
本研究解决了识别大型语言模型（LLMs）漏洞以提高其安全性的关键需求，特别关注越狱问题，即对手利用精心设计的提示绕过安全防护。以往的方法主要依赖于二元攻击成功率（ASR）信号或手动设计的评分模板，这两者都存在稀疏性和人为偏见等问题。提出的方法AMIS（Align to MISalign）引入了一种元优化框架，通过双层结构同时演变越狱提示和评分模板，有效解决了现有方法的局限性。本文的贡献在于证明提示和评分信号的共同优化可以提高性能，在Claude-3.5-Haiku上实现88.0%的ASR，在Claude-4-Sonnet上实现100.0%的完美ASR，从而支持通过更有效的越狱检测来增强LLM安全性的目标。
A Self-Improving Architecture for Dynamic Safety in Large Language Models
Authors: Tyler Slater
First: 2025-11-10T21:39:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T17:52:48+00:00
Comments: Under review at the journal Information and Software Technology (Special Issue on Software Architecture for AI-Driven Systems)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Context: Large Language Models (LLMs) rely on static, pre-deployment safety mechanisms that cannot adapt to adversarial threats discovered after release. Objective: To design a software architecture enabling LLM-based systems to autonomously detect safety failures and synthesize defense policies at runtime, without retraining or manual intervention. Method: We propose the Self-Improving Safety Framework (SISF), grounded in the MAPE-K reference model. The framework couples a target LLM with a feedback loop: an Adjudicator detects breaches, a Policy Synthesis Module generates dual-mechanism defense policies (heuristic and semantic), and a Warden enforces them. We conducted seven experiments (10,061 evaluations) across four model families. Results: Across five reproducibility trials, SISF achieved a mean Attack Success Rate (ASR) of 0.27% (+/-0.15%), autonomously generating 240 policies per trial. Cross-model evaluation confirmed deployment portability. A held-out test showed a 68.5% proactive interception rate on unseen attacks. Stacked behind Llama Guard 4, the combined defense reduced residual ASR from 7.88% to 0.00%. Ablation confirmed both heuristic and semantic policy types are architecturally required. Conclusion: Self-adaptive architecture is a viable approach to LLM safety. SISF achieves sub-1% ASR through synchronous output monitoring, progressively shifting enforcement to fast, local Warden policies via the MAPE-K loop, offering a new pattern for building resilient AI systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：用于大型语言模型动态安全的自我改进架构
背景：大型语言模型（LLMs）依赖于静态的、预部署的安全机制，这些机制无法适应发布后发现的对抗性威胁。目标：设计一种软件架构，使基于LLM的系统能够自主检测安全故障并在运行时合成防御策略，而无需重新训练或人工干预。方法：我们提出了自我改进安全框架（SISF），基于MAPE-K参考模型。该框架将目标LLM与反馈循环结合：裁决者检测违规，策略合成模块生成双机制防御策略（启发式和语义），守卫者执行这些策略。我们在四个模型系列中进行了七个实验（10,061次评估）。结果：在五次可重复性试验中，SISF实现了平均攻击成功率（ASR）为0.27%（+/-0.15%），每次试验自主生成240个策略。跨模型评估确认了部署的可移植性。保留测试显示在未见攻击上的主动拦截率为68.5%。在Llama Guard 4的支持下，组合防御将残余ASR从7.88%降低到0.00%。消融实验确认启发式和语义策略类型在架构上都是必需的。结论：自适应架构是LLM安全的可行方法。SISF通过同步输出监控实现了低于1%的ASR，逐步将执行转移到快速、本地的守卫者策略，通过MAPE-K循环，提供了一种构建弹性AI系统的新模式。

Previous methods lacked the ability to autonomously detect and respond to safety failures, necessitating manual intervention and retraining. The proposed Self-Improving Safety Framework (SISF) innovatively integrates a feedback loop with an Adjudicator, Policy Synthesis Module, and Warden to autonomously generate and enforce defense policies in real-time. This architecture was tested through seven experiments involving over 10,000 evaluations, achieving a mean Attack Success Rate (ASR) of 0.27% and a proactive interception rate of 68.5% on unseen attacks. The results demonstrate that SISF significantly enhances LLM safety, achieving sub-1% ASR and providing a robust framework for developing resilient AI systems.

Robust Multimodal Safety via Conditional Decoding
Authors: Anurag Kumar, Raghuveer Peri, Jon Burnsky, Alexandru Nelus, Rohit Paturi, Srikanth Vishnubhotla, Yanjun Qi
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-03-31T23:19:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T23:19:50+00:00
Comments: 8 pages + Appendix section. Submitted to ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multimodal large-language models (MLLMs) often experience degraded safety alignment when harmful queries exploit cross-modal interactions. Models aligned on text alone show a higher rate of successful attacks when extended to two or more modalities. In this work, we propose a simple conditional decoding strategy, CASA (Classification Augmented with Safety Attention) that utilizes internal representations of MLLMs to predict a binary safety token before response generation. We introduce a novel safety attention module designed to enhance the model's ability to detect malicious queries. Our design ensures robust safety alignment without relying on any external classifier or auxiliary head, and without the need for modality-specific safety fine-tuning. On diverse benchmarks such as MM-SafetyBench, JailbreakV-28k, and adversarial audio tests, CASA lowers the average attack success rate by more than 97% across modalities and across attack types. Our empirical evaluations also show that CASA maintains strong utility in benign inputs, a result validated through both automated and human evaluations (via 13 trained annotators). Together, these results highlight CASA as a simple and generalizable framework to improve multimodal LLM safety.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过条件解码实现稳健的多模态安全
多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在有害查询利用跨模态交互时，往往会出现安全对齐下降的情况。仅在文本上对齐的模型在扩展到两个或更多模态时，成功攻击的比率更高。在本研究中，我们提出了一种简单的条件解码策略CASA（带有安全注意力的分类增强），利用MLLMs的内部表示在生成响应之前预测二元安全标记。我们引入了一种新颖的安全注意力模块，旨在增强模型检测恶意查询的能力。我们的设计确保了稳健的安全对齐，无需依赖任何外部分类器或辅助头，也无需特定模态的安全微调。在MM-SafetyBench、JailbreakV-28k和对抗音频测试等多样化基准上，CASA在各模态和攻击类型中将平均攻击成功率降低了超过97%。我们的实证评估还表明，CASA在良性输入中保持强大的实用性，这一结果通过自动化和人工评估（通过13名训练过的注释员）得到了验证。这些结果共同突显了CASA作为一个简单且可推广的框架，以提高多模态LLM的安全性。

This research addresses the issue of safety alignment in multimodal large-language models (MLLMs), which often suffer from vulnerabilities when harmful queries exploit interactions between different modalities. Previous methods primarily focused on text alignment, leading to increased attack success rates when models were extended to multiple modalities. The proposed CASA (Classification Augmented with Safety Attention) approach introduces a conditional decoding strategy that leverages internal representations of MLLMs to predict a binary safety token prior to generating responses, incorporating a novel safety attention module to enhance malicious query detection. This method does not require external classifiers or modality-specific fine-tuning, making it a well-motivated solution to existing problems. The paper demonstrates that CASA significantly reduces the average attack success rate by over 97% across various benchmarks, including MM-SafetyBench and JailbreakV-28k, while maintaining strong performance on benign inputs, thus supporting its goals of improving multimodal LLM safety.

Colluding LoRA: A Compositional Vulnerability in LLM Safety Alignment
Authors: Sihao Ding
First: 2026-03-13T05:53:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-30T05:02:56+00:00
Comments: Updated manuscript to better reflect the core contribution
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We show that safety alignment in modular LLMs can exhibit a compositional vulnerability: adapters that appear benign and plausibly functional in isolation can, when linearly composed, compromise safety. We study this failure mode through Colluding LoRA (CoLoRA), in which harmful behavior emerges only in the composition state. Unlike attacks that depend on adversarial prompts or explicit input triggers, this composition-triggered broad refusal suppression causes the model to comply with harmful requests under standard prompts once a particular set of adapters is loaded. This behavior exposes a combinatorial blind spot in current unit-centric defenses, for which exhaustive verification over adapter compositions is computationally intractable. Across several open-weight LLMs, we find that individual adapters remain benign in isolation while their composition yields high attack success rates, indicating that securing modular LLM supply-chains requires moving beyond single-module verification toward composition-aware defenses.
中文标题/摘要
标题：共谋LoRA：LLM安全对齐中的组合脆弱性
我们展示了模块化LLM中的安全对齐可能表现出组合脆弱性：在孤立状态下看似良性且功能合理的适配器，在线性组合时可能会危害安全。我们通过共谋LoRA（CoLoRA）研究这种失效模式，其中有害行为仅在组合状态下出现。与依赖对抗性提示或显式输入触发的攻击不同，这种组合触发的广泛拒绝抑制导致模型在加载特定适配器集后，在标准提示下遵从有害请求。这种行为暴露了当前以单元为中心的防御中的组合盲点，全面验证适配器组合在计算上是不可行的。在多个开放权重的LLM中，我们发现单个适配器在孤立状态下保持良性，而它们的组合则产生高攻击成功率，这表明保护模块化LLM供应链需要超越单模块验证，朝着组合感知防御的方向发展。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the safety alignment issues in modular large language models (LLMs), highlighting a compositional vulnerability where seemingly benign adapters can lead to harmful behavior when combined. Previous methods focused on unit-centric defenses, which fail to account for the interactions between adapters, making them inadequate for ensuring safety in complex compositions. The proposed approach, Colluding LoRA (CoLoRA), emphasizes the need for composition-aware defenses that can identify and mitigate risks arising from adapter combinations. This study employs a methodology that tests various open-weight LLMs to reveal that while individual adapters appear safe, their combinations can significantly increase attack success rates. The findings underscore the necessity of evolving verification strategies to secure modular LLM supply chains effectively.
本研究探讨了模块化大型语言模型（LLMs）中的安全对齐脆弱性，特别关注看似无害的适配器在组合时可能导致有害行为。以往的方法主要依赖于单元中心的防御，验证单个适配器的安全性，但未能考虑其组合所带来的风险，从而在安全措施中留下了显著的盲点。提出的方法Colluding LoRA（CoLoRA）强调了组合感知防御的重要性，揭示了只有在某些适配器组合时，才会出现有害行为，因此需要转变验证策略。该方法论涉及对多种开放权重LLMs进行测试，表明虽然单个适配器是安全的，但其组合可能导致高攻击成功率。这一发现强调了在模块化LLM供应链中改善安全措施的必要性，支持了增强这些系统安全对齐的目标。
Enhancing Jailbreak Attacks on LLMs via Persona Prompts
Authors: Zheng Zhang, Peilin Zhao, Deheng Ye, Hao Wang
Venue: NeurIPS 2025
First: 2025-07-28T12:03:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T15:46:17+00:00
Comments: Workshop on LLM Persona Modeling at NeurIPS 2025
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Jailbreak attacks aim to exploit large language models (LLMs) by inducing them to generate harmful content, thereby revealing their vulnerabilities. Understanding and addressing these attacks is crucial for advancing the field of LLM safety. Previous jailbreak approaches have mainly focused on direct manipulations of harmful intent, with limited attention to the impact of persona prompts. In this study, we systematically explore the efficacy of persona prompts in compromising LLM defenses. We propose a genetic algorithm-based method that automatically crafts persona prompts to bypass LLM's safety mechanisms. Our experiments reveal that: (1) our evolved persona prompts reduce refusal rates by 50-70% across multiple LLMs, and (2) these prompts demonstrate synergistic effects when combined with existing attack methods, increasing success rates by 10-20%. Our code and data are available at https://github.com/CjangCjengh/Generic_Persona.

SafeSeek: Universal Attribution of Safety Circuits in Language Models
Authors: Miao Yu, Siyuan Fu, Moayad Aloqaily, Zhenhong Zhou, Safa Otoum, Xing fan, Kun Wang, Yufei Guo, Qingsong Wen
First: 2026-03-24T14:32:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T14:32:53+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Mechanistic interpretability reveals that safety-critical behaviors (e.g., alignment, jailbreak, backdoor) in Large Language Models (LLMs) are grounded in specialized functional components. However, existing safety attribution methods struggle with generalization and reliability due to their reliance on heuristic, domain-specific metrics and search algorithms. To address this, we propose \ourmethod, a unified safety interpretability framework that identifies functionally complete safety circuits in LLMs via optimization. Unlike methods focusing on isolated heads or neurons, \ourmethod introduces differentiable binary masks to extract multi-granular circuits through gradient descent on safety datasets, while integrates Safety Circuit Tuning to utilize these sparse circuits for efficient safety fine-tuning. We validate \ourmethod in two key scenarios in LLM safety: \textbf{(1) backdoor attacks}, identifying a backdoor circuit with 0.42\% sparsity, whose ablation eradicates the Attack Success Rate (ASR) from 100\% $\to$ 0.4\% while retaining over 99\% general utility; \textbf{(2) safety alignment}, localizing an alignment circuit with 3.03\% heads and 0.79\% neurons, whose removal spikes ASR from 0.8\% $\to$ 96.9\%, whereas excluding this circuit during helpfulness fine-tuning maintains 96.5\% safety retention.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SafeSeek：语言模型中安全电路的通用归因
机械解释性揭示了大型语言模型（LLMs）中安全关键行为（例如，调整、越狱、后门）是基于专门的功能组件。然而，现有的安全归因方法由于依赖启发式、特定领域的指标和搜索算法，难以实现泛化和可靠性。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了\ourmethod，一个统一的安全可解释性框架，通过优化识别LLMs中的功能完整安全电路。与专注于孤立头部或神经元的方法不同，\ourmethod引入可微分的二进制掩码，通过对安全数据集的梯度下降提取多粒度电路，同时集成安全电路调优，以利用这些稀疏电路进行高效的安全微调。我们在LLM安全的两个关键场景中验证了\ourmethod：\textbf{(1) 后门攻击}，识别出一个稀疏度为0.42\%的后门电路，其消融使攻击成功率（ASR）从100\%降至0.4\%，同时保留超过99\%的通用效用；\textbf{(2) 安全对齐}，定位一个稀疏度为3.03\%的对齐电路和0.79\%的神经元，其移除使ASR从0.8\%激增至96.9\%，而在有用性微调中排除该电路则保持96.5\%的安全保留。

DriveSafe: A Hierarchical Risk Taxonomy for Safety-Critical LLM-Based Driving Assistants
Authors: Abhishek Kumar, Riya Tapwal, Carsten Maple
First: 2026-01-17T18:50:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T18:19:05+00:00
Comments: This is the revised version of the paper
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly integrated into vehicle-based digital assistants, where unsafe, ambiguous, or legally incorrect responses can lead to serious safety, ethical, and regulatory consequences. Despite growing interest in LLM safety, existing taxonomies and evaluation frameworks remain largely general-purpose and fail to capture the domain-specific risks inherent to real-world driving scenarios. In this paper, we introduce DriveSafe, a hierarchical, four-level risk taxonomy designed to systematically characterize safety-critical failure modes of LLM-based driving assistants. The taxonomy comprises 129 fine-grained atomic risk categories spanning technical, legal, societal, and ethical dimensions, grounded in real-world driving regulations and safety principles and reviewed by domain experts. To validate the safety relevance and realism of the constructed prompts, we evaluate their refusal behavior across six widely deployed LLMs. Our analysis shows that the evaluated models often fail to appropriately refuse unsafe or non-compliant driving-related queries, underscoring the limitations of general-purpose safety alignment in driving contexts.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DriveSafe：安全关键型基于LLM的驾驶助手的分层风险分类法

Using LLM-as-a-Judge/Jury to Advance Scalable, Clinically-Validated Safety Evaluations of Model Responses to Users Demonstrating Psychosis
Authors: May Lynn Reese, Markela Zeneli, Mindy Ng, Jacob Haimes, Andreea Damien, Elizabeth Stade
Venue: NeurIPS 2025
First: 2026-03-20T04:31:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-20T04:31:03+00:00
Comments: published at IASEAI 2026, preliminary work presented at GenAI4Health workshop at NeurIPS 2025
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
General-purpose Large Language Models (LLMs) are becoming widely adopted by people for mental health support. Yet emerging evidence suggests there are significant risks associated with high-frequency use, particularly for individuals suffering from psychosis, as LLMs may reinforce delusions and hallucinations. Existing evaluations of LLMs in mental health contexts are limited by a lack of clinical validation and scalability of assessment. To address these issues, this research focuses on psychosis as a critical condition for LLM safety evaluation by (1) developing and validating seven clinician-informed safety criteria, (2) constructing a human-consensus dataset, and (3) testing automated assessment using an LLM as an evaluator (LLM-as-a-Judge) or taking the majority vote of several LLM judges (LLM-as-a-Jury). Results indicate that LLM-as-a-Judge aligns closely with the human consensus (Cohen's $κ_{\text{human} \times \text{gemini}} = 0.75$, $κ_{\text{human} \times \text{qwen}} = 0.68$, $κ_{\text{human} \times \text{kimi}} = 0.56$) and that the best judge slightly outperforms LLM-as-a-Jury (Cohen's $κ_{\text{human} \times \text{jury}} = 0.74$). Overall, these findings have promising implications for clinically grounded, scalable methods in LLM safety evaluations for mental health contexts.
中文标题/摘要
标题：使用LLM作为评判者/陪审团推进可扩展的临床验证模型响应用户精神病的安全评估
通用大型语言模型（LLMs）正被广泛应用于心理健康支持。然而， emerging evidence表明，高频使用存在显著风险，尤其是对精神病患者，因为LLMs可能会强化妄想和幻觉。现有的LLMs在心理健康背景下的评估受限于缺乏临床验证和评估的可扩展性。为了解决这些问题，本研究将精神病作为LLM安全评估的关键条件，(1) 开发并验证七个临床知情的安全标准，(2) 构建人类共识数据集，(3) 测试使用LLM作为评估者的自动化评估（LLM作为评判者）或采取多个LLM评判者的多数投票（LLM作为陪审团）。结果表明，LLM作为评判者与人类共识高度一致（Cohen's $κ_{\text{human} \times \text{gemini}} = 0.75$, $κ_{\text{human} \times \text{qwen}} = 0.68$, $κ_{\text{human} \times \text{kimi}} = 0.56$），而最佳评判者略微优于LLM作为陪审团（Cohen's $κ_{\text{human} \times \text{jury}} = 0.74$）。总体而言，这些发现对心理健康背景下LLM安全评估的临床基础和可扩展方法具有良好的启示。

LISAA: A Framework for Large Language Model Information Security Awareness Assessment
Authors: Ofir Cohen, Gil Ari Agmon, Asaf Shabtai, Rami Puzis
First: 2024-11-20T11:09:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T22:34:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The popularity of large language models (LLMs) continues to grow, and LLM-based assistants have become ubiquitous. Information security awareness (ISA) is an important yet underexplored area of LLM safety. ISA encompasses LLMs' security knowledge, which has been explored in the past, as well as their attitudes and behaviors, which are crucial to LLMs' ability to understand implicit security context and reject unsafe requests that may cause an LLM to unintentionally fail the user. We introduce LISAA, a comprehensive framework to assess LLM ISA. The proposed framework applies an automated measurement method to a comprehensive set of 100 realistic scenarios covering all security topics in an ISA taxonomy. These scenarios create tension between implicit security implications and user satisfaction. Applying our LISAA framework to leading LLMs highlights a widespread vulnerability affecting current deployments: many popular models exhibit only medium to low ISA levels, exposing their users to cybersecurity threats, and models that rank highly in cybersecurity knowledge benchmarks sometimes achieve relatively low ISA ranking. In addition, we found that smaller variants of the same model family are significantly riskier. Furthermore, while newer model versions demonstrated notable improvements, meaningful gaps in their ISA persist, suggesting that there is room for improvement. We release an online tool that implements our framework and enables the evaluation of new models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LISAA：大型语言模型信息安全意识评估框架
大型语言模型（LLMs）的普及持续增长，基于LLM的助手已变得无处不在。信息安全意识（ISA）是LLM安全性的重要但未充分探索的领域。ISA包括LLM的安全知识，这在过去已有研究，以及它们的态度和行为，这对LLM理解隐含安全上下文和拒绝可能导致LLM无意中未能满足用户的安全请求至关重要。我们介绍了LISAA，一个全面评估LLM ISA的框架。该框架应用自动测量方法，涵盖ISA分类法中所有安全主题的100个现实场景。这些场景在隐含安全影响和用户满意度之间产生紧张关系。将我们的LISAA框架应用于领先的LLM，突显了当前部署中普遍存在的脆弱性：许多流行模型的ISA水平仅为中等到低，暴露其用户于网络安全威胁中，而在网络安全知识基准中排名较高的模型有时在ISA排名中相对较低。此外，我们发现同一模型家族的小型变体风险显著更高。此外，尽管较新版本的模型表现出显著改善，但它们的ISA仍存在显著差距，表明仍有改进空间。我们发布了一个在线工具，实施我们的框架并支持新模型的评估。

An online tool implementing this framework has been released to facilitate the evaluation of new models.

Efficient LLM Safety Evaluation through Multi-Agent Debate
Authors: Dachuan Lin, Guobin Shen, Zihao Yang, Tianrong Liu, Dongcheng Zhao, Yi Zeng
First: 2025-11-09T14:06:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T02:09:28+00:00
Comments: 15 pages, 5 figures, 10 tables. Updated abstract to fix an incconsistency issue with the main paper: HAJailBench size (12,000 -> 11,100)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety evaluation of large language models (LLMs) increasingly relies on LLM-as-a-judge pipelines, but strong judges can still be expensive to use at scale. We study whether structured multi-agent debate can improve judge reliability while keeping backbone size and cost modest. To do so, we introduce HAJailBench, a human-annotated jailbreak benchmark with 11,100 labeled interactions spanning diverse attack methods and target models, and we pair it with a Multi-Agent Judge framework in which critic, defender, and judge agents debate under a shared safety rubric. On HAJailBench, the framework improves over matched small-model prompt baselines and prior multi-agent judges, while remaining more economical than GPT-4o under the evaluated pricing snapshot. Ablation results further show that a small number of debate rounds is sufficient to capture most of the gain. Together, these results support structured, value-aligned debate as a practical design for scalable LLM safety evaluation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过多智能体辩论实现高效的LLM安全评估
大型语言模型（LLMs）的安全评估越来越依赖于LLM作为评审的管道，但强大的评审在大规模使用时仍然成本高昂。我们研究结构化的多智能体辩论是否能在保持骨干规模和成本适中的同时提高评审的可靠性。为此，我们引入了HAJailBench，这是一个人类注释的越狱基准，包含11,100个标记的交互，涵盖多种攻击方法和目标模型，并将其与多智能体评审框架配对，在该框架中，批评者、防御者和评审代理在共享的安全标准下进行辩论。在HAJailBench上，该框架在匹配的小模型提示基线和先前的多智能体评审中表现更好，同时在评估的定价快照下仍然比GPT-4o更经济。消融结果进一步表明，少量的辩论轮次足以捕捉大部分增益。综合来看，这些结果支持结构化、价值对齐的辩论作为可扩展LLM安全评估的实用设计。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the growing need for effective safety evaluation of large language models (LLMs), which traditionally relies on expensive LLM-as-a-judge pipelines. Previous methods have struggled with high costs and reliability issues, prompting the authors to propose a structured multi-agent debate approach that maintains modest backbone size and cost. This approach is well-motivated as it aims to enhance judge reliability while being more economical than existing solutions like GPT-4o. The paper introduces HAJailBench, a benchmark with 11,100 labeled interactions, and employs a Multi-Agent Judge framework where critic, defender, and judge agents engage in debate. The findings demonstrate that this framework outperforms previous methods on HAJailBench and shows that a limited number of debate rounds can achieve significant improvements, supporting the practicality of structured debate for scalable LLM safety evaluation.
本研究解决了对大型语言模型（LLMs）进行有效安全评估的日益需求，传统方法依赖于成本高昂且效率低下的LLM作为评判者的管道。以往的方法通常依赖于单一评判者或较不结构化的方式，导致可靠性和高运营成本的问题。所提出的方法引入了HAJailBench，这是一个包含11,100个标注交互的人类注释基准，并采用多代理评判框架，其中批评者、防御者和评判者在结构化辩论中进行互动，以增强可靠性，同时保持成本效益。该方法的动机明确，旨在为LLM安全评估提供可扩展的解决方案。该方法论表明，多代理辩论框架在HAJailBench基准上优于以往模型和方法，在实现更高性能的同时，比现有解决方案如GPT-4o更具经济性，从而支持可扩展安全评估的目标。
SFCoT: Safer Chain-of-Thought via Active Safety Evaluation and Calibration
Authors: Yu Pan, Wenlong Yu, Tiejun Wu, Xiaohu Ye, Qiannan Si, Guangquan Xu, Bin Wu
First: 2026-03-16T15:13:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T15:13:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable capabilities in complex reasoning tasks. However, they remain highly susceptible to jailbreak attacks that undermine their safety alignment. Existing defense mechanisms typically rely on post hoc filtering applied only to the final output, leaving intermediate reasoning steps unmonitored and vulnerable to adversarial manipulation. To address this gap, this paper proposes a SaFer Chain-of-Thought (SFCoT) framework, which proactively evaluates and calibrates potentially unsafe reasoning steps in real time. SFCoT incorporates a three-tier safety scoring system alongside a multi-perspective consistency verification mechanism, designed to detect potential risks throughout the reasoning process. A dynamic intervention module subsequently performs targeted calibration to redirect reasoning trajectories toward safe outcomes. Experimental results demonstrate that SFCoT reduces the attack success rate from $58.97\%$ to $12.31\%$, demonstrating it as an effective and efficient LLM safety enhancement method without a significant decline in general performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SFCoT：通过主动安全评估和校准实现更安全的思维链
大型语言模型（LLMs）在复杂推理任务中表现出显著能力。然而，它们仍然高度易受破坏攻击，削弱了其安全对齐。现有的防御机制通常依赖于仅应用于最终输出的事后过滤，导致中间推理步骤未被监控，易受对抗性操控。为了解决这一问题，本文提出了一种更安全的思维链（SFCoT）框架，能够实时主动评估和校准潜在不安全的推理步骤。SFCoT结合了三级安全评分系统和多角度一致性验证机制，旨在检测推理过程中的潜在风险。动态干预模块随后执行针对性校准，以将推理轨迹引导向安全结果。实验结果表明，SFCoT将攻击成功率从58.97%降低到12.31%，证明其作为一种有效且高效的LLM安全增强方法，且未显著降低整体性能。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the vulnerability of large language models (LLMs) to jailbreak attacks that compromise their safety alignment, a significant concern given their capabilities in complex reasoning tasks. Previous methods primarily focused on post hoc filtering of final outputs, which left intermediate reasoning steps unprotected and susceptible to adversarial manipulation. The proposed SaFer Chain-of-Thought (SFCoT) framework differs by actively evaluating and calibrating potentially unsafe reasoning steps in real time, utilizing a three-tier safety scoring system and a multi-perspective consistency verification mechanism to identify risks throughout the reasoning process. The contribution of this paper lies in its innovative approach to enhancing LLM safety without sacrificing overall performance, as evidenced by experimental results showing a reduction in attack success rates from 58.97% to 12.31%, indicating that the method effectively supports its safety enhancement goals while maintaining general performance levels.
本研究关注大型语言模型（LLMs）在越狱攻击下的脆弱性，这些攻击会破坏其安全对齐。以往的方法主要集中在对最终输出进行事后过滤，未能监控中间推理步骤，从而使其暴露于对抗性操控之下。提出的安全链式思维（SFCoT）框架通过实时主动评估和校准推理步骤而有所不同，利用三层安全评分系统和多角度一致性验证机制识别推理过程中的风险。这种方法的动机充分，因为它在不显著影响整体性能的情况下增强了安全性。该方法论包括一个动态干预模块，用于重新校准推理轨迹，实验结果表明，SFCoT有效地将攻击成功率从58.97%降低到12.31%，支持其提高LLM安全性的目标。
From Evaluation to Defense: Advancing Safety in Video Large Language Models
Authors: Yiwei Sun, Peiqi Jiang, Chuanbin Liu, Luohao Lin, Zhiying Lu, Hongtao Xie
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-05-22T13:16:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T13:05:37+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
While the safety risks of image-based large language models (Image LLMs) have been extensively studied, their video-based counterparts (Video LLMs) remain critically under-examined. To systematically study this problem, we introduce VideoSafetyEval - a large-scale, real-world benchmark for Video LLM safety, which comprises 11.4k video-query pairs and spans 19 principal risk categories. Based on this, we reveal that integrating video modality degrades safety performance by an average of 34.2%, thereby exposing systemic risks in multimodal attack exploitation. To address this vulnerability, we propose VideoSafety-R1, a dual-stage framework achieving unprecedented safety gains through three innovations: (1) the VideoSafetyThinking dataset contains 46k video-query-thinking response triplets; (2) Alarm Token-Guided Safety Fine-Tuning (AT-SFT) injects learnable alarm tokens into visual and textual sequences, enabling explicit harm perception across modalities via multitask objectives; and (3) safety-guided GRPO enhances defensive reasoning through dynamic policy optimization with rule-based rewards derived from dual-modality verification. These components synergize to shift safety alignment from harm perception to active reasoning. The framework achieves a 71.1% improvement on VSE-HH, and improves by 59.1%, 44.3%, and 15.0% on the image safety datasets MMBench, VLGuard, and FigStep, respectively. Our code and dataset are available at https://github.com/Emiya-syw/VideoSafety-R1.git. Note: This paper contains harmful language and image examples, and reader discretion is recommended.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从评估到防御：提升视频大型语言模型的安全性
尽管基于图像的大型语言模型（图像LLM）的安全风险已被广泛研究，但其视频基础的对应模型（视频LLM）仍然缺乏系统性研究。为系统性研究这一问题，我们引入了VideoSafetyEval——一个针对视频LLM安全性的大规模真实基准，包含11.4k视频-查询对，涵盖19个主要风险类别。基于此，我们揭示了视频模态的整合使安全性能平均下降34.2%，从而暴露了多模态攻击利用中的系统性风险。为了解决这一脆弱性，我们提出了VideoSafety-R1，一个通过三项创新实现前所未有的安全提升的双阶段框架：（1）VideoSafetyThinking数据集包含46k视频-查询-思考响应三元组；（2）报警令牌引导的安全微调（AT-SFT）将可学习的报警令牌注入视觉和文本序列，通过多任务目标实现跨模态的明确伤害感知；（3）安全引导的GRPO通过基于规则的奖励增强防御推理，动态优化策略，基于双模态验证。这些组件协同作用，将安全对齐从伤害感知转向主动推理。该框架在VSE-HH上实现了71.1%的提升，并在图像安全数据集MMBench、VLGuard和FigStep上分别提高了59.1%、44.3%和15.0%。我们的代码和数据集可在https://github.com/Emiya-syw/VideoSafety-R1.git获取。注意：本文包含有害语言和图像示例，建议读者谨慎阅读。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the critical safety risks associated with video-based large language models (Video LLMs), which have not been thoroughly examined compared to their image-based counterparts. Previous methods have largely overlooked the unique challenges posed by video modalities, leading to a significant degradation in safety performance, as evidenced by a 34.2% average decline in safety metrics. The proposed approach, VideoSafety-R1, introduces a dual-stage framework that includes the VideoSafetyThinking dataset, Alarm Token-Guided Safety Fine-Tuning (AT-SFT), and safety-guided GRPO, effectively enhancing safety alignment through active reasoning rather than mere harm perception. The methodology demonstrates substantial improvements in safety performance, achieving a 71.1% increase on the VSE-HH task and notable enhancements on several image safety datasets, thereby supporting the goal of advancing safety in Video LLMs.
本文探讨了视频大型语言模型（Video LLMs）中未充分研究的安全风险，与对图像大型语言模型的广泛研究形成对比。以往的方法未能充分解决Video LLMs独特的脆弱性，尤其是在整合视频模态时安全性能平均下降34.2%。提出的方法VideoSafety-R1引入了一个双阶段框架，通过三个关键创新来增强安全性：VideoSafetyThinking数据集、基于警报标记的安全微调（AT-SFT）和安全引导的GRPO。这种方法将重点从单纯感知危害转向主动推理安全，在VSE-HH任务上实现了71.1%的提升，并在多个图像安全数据集上取得显著进展，证明了其在增强Video LLMs安全性方面的有效性。
OffTopicEval: When Large Language Models Enter the Wrong Chat, Almost Always!
Authors: Jingdi Lei, Varun Gumma, Rishabh Bhardwaj, Seok Min Lim, Chuan Li, Amir Zadeh, Soujanya Poria
First: 2025-09-30T16:39:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-13T11:01:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Model (LLM) safety is one of the most pressing challenges for enabling wide-scale deployment. While most studies and global discussions focus on generic harms, such as models assisting users in harming themselves or others, enterprises face a more fundamental concern: whether LLM-based agents are safe for their intended use case. To address this, we introduce operational safety, defined as an LLM's ability to appropriately accept or refuse user queries when tasked with a specific purpose. We further propose OffTopicEval, an evaluation suite and benchmark for measuring operational safety both in general and within specific agentic use cases. Our evaluations on six model families comprising 20 open-weight LLMs reveal that while performance varies across models, all of them remain highly operationally unsafe. Even the strongest models - Qwen-3 (235B) with 77.77% and Mistral (24B) with 79.96% - fall far short of reliable operational safety, while GPT models plateau in the 62-73% range, Phi achieves only mid-level scores (48-70%), and Gemma and Llama-3 collapse to 39.53% and 23.84%, respectively. While operational safety is a core model alignment issue, to suppress these failures, we propose prompt-based steering methods: query grounding (Q-ground) and system-prompt grounding (P-ground), which substantially improve OOD refusal. Q-ground provides consistent gains of up to 23%, while P-ground delivers even larger boosts, raising Llama-3.3 (70B) by 41% and Qwen-3 (30B) by 27%. These results highlight both the urgent need for operational safety interventions and the promise of prompt-based steering as a first step toward more reliable LLM-based agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：OffTopicEval：当大型语言模型进入错误的聊天时，几乎总是如此！
大型语言模型（LLM）安全性是实现大规模部署面临的最紧迫挑战之一。虽然大多数研究和全球讨论集中在一般性危害上，例如模型帮助用户伤害自己或他人，但企业面临更根本的担忧：基于LLM的代理是否安全用于其预期用途。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了操作安全性，定义为LLM在特定目的下适当地接受或拒绝用户查询的能力。我们进一步提出了OffTopicEval，一个评估套件和基准，用于测量一般和特定代理使用案例中的操作安全性。我们对六个模型家族中20个开放权重LLM的评估显示，尽管模型之间的性能差异很大，但它们都高度操作不安全。即使是最强的模型 - Qwen-3（235B）得分77.77%和Mistral（24B）得分79.96% - 也远未达到可靠的操作安全性，而GPT模型的得分停留在62-73%范围内，Phi仅获得中等得分（48-70%），Gemma和Llama-3分别降至39.53%和23.84%。虽然操作安全性是核心模型对齐问题，为了抑制这些失败，我们提出了基于提示的引导方法：查询基础（Q-ground）和系统提示基础（P-ground），显著提高了OOD拒绝率。Q-ground提供了高达23%的持续增益，而P-ground则提供了更大的提升，将Llama-3.3（70B）提高了41%，将Qwen-3（30B）提高了27%。这些结果突显了对操作安全性干预的迫切需求，以及基于提示的引导作为朝着更可靠的基于LLM的代理迈出的第一步的前景。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the critical challenge of safety in deploying Large Language Models (LLMs), particularly focusing on operational safety, which is the ability of LLMs to appropriately handle user queries for specific purposes. Previous methods primarily concentrated on generic harms, neglecting the specific context of LLM usage, leading to a lack of reliable operational safety across various models. The proposed OffTopicEval evaluation suite aims to measure operational safety in both general and specific contexts, revealing that all tested models exhibit significant operational safety issues, with the best-performing models still falling short of acceptable standards. The methodology includes prompt-based steering techniques, specifically query grounding (Q-ground) and system-prompt grounding (P-ground), which enhance out-of-distribution refusal rates, achieving notable performance improvements. The findings underscore the necessity for operational safety measures and demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed methods, with Q-ground and P-ground yielding performance gains of up to 41% and 27%, respectively, indicating a promising direction for developing safer LLM-based agents.
